                  <li class="menu-item wpmm-type-widget menu-widget-class wpmm-type-widget wp-megamenu-item-55971 wpmm-submenu-right">

                    <h2>
                     Our Mission
                    </h2>
                    <div class="items">
                     <div class="item">
                      <div class="media-wrapper">
                       <img alt="" class="lazyload" src="https://oceanconservancy.org/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/seal-compressed.gif"/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="text-wrapper">
                       <p>
                        Ocean Conservancy is working with you to protect the ocean from today’s greatest global challenges. Together, we create science-based solutions for a healthy ocean and the wildlife and communities that depend on it.
                       </p>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                   </div>

            <script>
             function toggleMute() {
    var video = document.getElementById("vimeo_video");
    var videoBtn = document.getElementById("vimeo_button");

    if (video.muted) {
        video.muted = false;
        videoBtn.classList.remove('on');
    } else {
        video.muted = true;
        videoBtn.classList.add('on');
    }
    return false;
}

                </h1>

              <section class="reef">
               <div class="reef__inner">
                <article class="buoy">
                 <header class="buoy__hed">
                  <h6 class="buoy__hed--sub">
                   Programs
                  </h6>
                  <h2 class="buoy__hed--hed">
                   Protecting the Arctic
                  </h2>
                 </header>
                 <p class="buoy--lede">
                  The Arctic is among the most spectacularly beautiful places on the planet—and one of the most remote. People have made their homes in this harsh region for millennia, and residents of Arctic coastal communities continue to rely on a healthy ocean to sustain a traditional way of life and as a vital source of food security.
                 </p>
                 <a class="action action--white" href="protecting-the-arctic">
                  Learn more
                 </a>
                </article>
                <blockquote class="reef__body">
                 <p class="reef__body--lede">
                  Protecting the Arctic should be an immediate priority for all nations of the world!
                 </p>
                 <div class="reef__body--author">
                  Whit Sheard, Senior Director, Shipping Emissions
                 </div>
                </blockquote>
               </div>
               <div class="reef__image">
                <picture>
                 <!--[if IE 9]><video style="display: none;"><![endif]-->
                 <source data-srcset="https://oceanconservancy.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/arctic-1-1200x814.jpg 1x, https://oceanconservancy.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/arctic-1.jpg 2x" media="(min-width: 900px)">
                  <source data-srcset="https://oceanconservancy.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/arctic-1-800x543.jpg 1x, https://oceanconservancy.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/arctic-1-1600x1086.jpg 2x" media="(min-width: 600px)">
                   <source data-srcset="https://oceanconservancy.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/arctic-1-640x434.jpg 1x, https://oceanconservancy.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/arctic-1-1280x869.jpg 2x" media="(min-width: 0px)">
                    <!--[if IE 9]></video><![endif]-->
                    <img alt="Protecting The Arctic" class="lazyload" data-srcset="https://oceanconservancy.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/arctic-1.jpg"/>
                    <noscript>
                     <img alt="Protecting The Arctic" class="lazyload" data-srcset="https://oceanconservancy.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/arctic-1.jpg"/>
                    </noscript>
                   </source>
                  </source>
                 </source>
                </picture>
               </div>
